href="/wiki/File:Bailarines.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Dancers with typical costume in El Tamaduste (<a href="/wiki/El_Hierro" title="El Hierro">El Hierro</a>).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Banda_de_Agaete_en_la_Tra%C3%ADda_del_Agua.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="320" decoding="async" height="255" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Banda_de_Agaete_en_la_Tra%C3%ADda_del_Agua.jpg/170px-Banda_de_Agaete_en_la_Tra%C3%ADda_del_Agua.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Banda_de_Agaete_en_la_Tra%C3%ADda_del_Agua.jpg/255px-Banda_de_Agaete_en_la_Tra%C3%ADda_del_Agua.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/78/Banda_de_Agaete_en_la_Tra%C3%ADda_del_Agua.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Banda_de_Agaete_en_la_Tra%C3%ADda_del_Agua.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Band of <a href="/wiki/Agaete" title="Agaete">Agaete</a> in the <i>Tra&#237;da del Agua</i> (<a href="/wiki/Gran_Canaria" title="Gran Canaria">Gran Canaria</a>).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Desfile_del_S%C3%A1bado_de_Carnaval,_en_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3672" data-file-width="4896" decoding="async" height="128" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Desfile_del_S%C3%A1bado_de_Carnaval%2C_en_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife.JPG/170px-Desfile_del_S%C3%A1bado_de_Carnaval%2C_en_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Desfile_del_S%C3%A1bado_de_Carnaval%2C_en_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife.JPG/255px-Desfile_del_S%C3%A1bado_de_Carnaval%2C_en_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Desfile_del_S%C3%A1bado_de_Carnaval%2C_en_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife.JPG/340px-Desfile_del_S%C3%A1bado_de_Carnaval%2C_en_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife.JPG 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Desfile_del_S%C3%A1bado_de_Carnaval,_en_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Parade in the <a href="/wiki/Carnival_of_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife" title="Carnival of Santa Cruz de Tenerife">Carnival of Santa Cruz de Tenerife</a>.</div></div></div>\n<p>Some holidays of those celebrated in the Canary Islands are international and national, others are regional holidays and others are of insular character. The official day of the autonomous community is <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canary_Islands_Day" title="Canary Islands Day">Canary Islands Day</a> on 30 May. The anniversary of the first session of the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_the_Canary_Islands" title="Parliament of the Canary Islands">Parliament of the Canary Islands</a>, based in the city of <a href="/wiki/Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife" title="Santa Cruz de Tenerife">Santa Cruz de Tenerife</a>, held on 30 May 1983, is commemorated with this day.\n</p><p>The common festive calendar throughout the Canary Islands is as follows:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105"><a href="#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<center>\n<table class="wikitable sortable" style="text-align:center;">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th width="120">Date\n</th>\n<th width="70">Name\n</th>\n<th width="250">Data\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>1 January</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/New_Year" title="New Year">New Year</a></td>\n<td>International festival.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>6 January</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Epiphany_(holiday)" title="Epiphany (holiday)">Epiphany</a></td>\n<td>Catholic festival.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>March or April</td>\n<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Holy_Thursday" title="Holy Thursday">Holy Thursday</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Holy_Friday" title="Holy Friday">Holy Friday</a></td>\n<td>Christian festival.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>1 May</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/International_Workers%27_Day" title="International Workers\' Day">International Workers\' Day</a></td>\n<td>International festival.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>30 May</td>\n<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canary_Islands_Day" title="Canary Islands Day">Canary Islands Day</a></td>\n<td>Day of the autonomous community. Anniversary of the first session of the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_the_Canary_Islands" title="Parliament of the Canary Islands">Parliament of the Canary Islands</a>.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>15 August</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Assumption_of_Mary" title="Assumption of Mary">Assumption of Mary</a></td>\n<td>Catholic festival. This day is festive in the archipelago as in all of Spain. Popularly, in the Canary Islands it is known as the day on which the is celebrated of <a href="/wiki/Virgin_of_Candelaria" title="Virgin of Candelaria">Virgin of Candelaria</a> (Saint Patron of the Canary Islands).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106"><a href="#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107"><a href="#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>12 October</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Fiesta_Nacional_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="Fiesta Nacional de Espa&#241;a">Fiesta Nacional de Espa&#241;a</a> (<i>D&#237;a de la Hispanidad</i>)</td>\n<td>National Holiday of Spain. Commemoration of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Discovery_of_the_Americas" title="Discovery of the Americas">discovery of the Americas</a>.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>1 November</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/All_Saints%27_Day" title="All Saints\' Day">All Saints\' Day</a></td>\n<td>Catholic festival.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>6 December</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Constitution_Day" title="Constitution Day">Constitution Day</a></td>\n<td>Commemoration of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spanish_constitutional_referendum,_1978" title="Spanish constitutional referendum, 1978">Spanish constitutional referendum, 1978</a>.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>8 December</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Immaculate_Conception" title="Immaculate Conception">Immaculate Conception</a></td>\n<td>Catholic festival. The Immaculate Conception is the Saint Patron of Spain.\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>25 December</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a></td>\n<td>Christian festival. Commemoration of the birth of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jesus_of_Nazareth" title="Jesus of Nazareth">Jesus of Nazareth</a>.\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n</center>\n<p>In addition, each of the islands has an island festival in which it is a holiday only on that island in question. These are the festivities of island patrons saints of each island. Organized chronologically are:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<center>\n<table class="wikitable sortable" style="text-align:center;">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th width="120">Date\n</th>\n<th width="70">Island\n</th>\n<th width="250">Saint/Virgin\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>2 February</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Tenerife" title="Tenerife">Tenerife</a></td>\n<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Our_Lady_of_Candelaria" title="Our Lady of Candelaria">Our Lady of Candelaria</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>5 August</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/La_Palma" title="La Palma">La Palma</a></td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Dedication_of_the_Basilica_of_St_Mary_Major" title="Dedication of the Basilica of St Mary Major">Our Lady of the Snows</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>8 September</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Gran_Canaria" title="Gran Canaria">Gran Canaria</a></td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Virgen_del_Pino" title="Virgen del Pino">Our Lady of the Pine</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>15 September</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Lanzarote" title="Lanzarote">Lanzarote</a></td>\n<td><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Our_Lady_of_Dolours&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Our Lady of Dolours (page does not exist)">Our Lady of Dolours</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Third Saturday of the month of September</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Fuerteventura" title="Fuerteventura">Fuerteventura</a></td>\n<td><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Our_Lady_of_the_Pe%C3%B1a&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Our Lady of the Pe&#241;a (page does not exist)">Our Lady of the Pe&#241;a</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>24 September</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/El_Hierro" title="El Hierro">El Hierro</a></td>\n<td><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Our_Lady_of_the_Kings&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Our Lady of the Kings (page does not exist)">Our Lady of the Kings</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Monday following the first Saturday of October</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/La_Gomera" title="La Gomera">La Gomera</a></td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Our_Lady_of_Guadalupe" title="Our Lady of Guadalupe">Our Lady of Guadalupe</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n</center>\n<p>The most famous festivals of the Canary Islands is the carnival. It is the most famous and international festival of the archipelago. The carnival is celebrated in all the islands and all its municipalities, perhaps the two busiest are those of the two Canarian capitals; the <a href="/wiki/Carnival_of_Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife" title="Carnival of Santa Cruz de Tenerife">Carnival of Santa Cruz de Tenerife</a> (<i>Tourist Festival of International Interest</i>) and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Carnival_of_Las_Palmas_de_Gran_Canaria" title="Carnival of Las Palmas de Gran Canaria">Carnival of Las Palmas de Gran Canaria</a>. It is celebrated on the streets between the months of February and March. But the rest of the islands of the archipelago have their carnivals with their own traditions among which stand out: The Festival of the Carneros of <a href="/wiki/El_Hierro" title="El Hierro">El Hierro</a>, the Festival of the Diabletes of <a href="/wiki/Teguise_(municipality)" title="Teguise (municipality)">Teguise</a> in <a href="/wiki/Lanzarote" title="Lanzarote">Lanzarote</a>, Los Indianos de <a href="/wiki/La_Palma" title="La Palma">La Palma</a>, the Carnival of <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n_de_La_Gomera" title="San Sebasti&#225;n de La Gomera">San Sebasti&#225;n de La Gomera</a> and the Carnival of <a href="/wiki/Puerto_del_Rosario" title="Puerto del Rosario">Puerto del Rosario</a> in <a href="/wiki/Fuerteventura" title="Fuerteventura">Fuerteventura</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Science_and_technology">Science and technology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Canary_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Science and technology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Erdfunkstelle_Gran_Canaria-3.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1235" data-file-width="3000" decoding="async" height="91" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Erdfunkstelle_Gran_Canaria-3.JPG/220px-Erdfunkstelle_Gran_Canaria-3.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Erdfunkstelle_Gran_Canaria-3.JPG/330px-Erdfunkstelle_Gran_Canaria-3.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Erdfunkstelle_Gran_Canaria-3.JPG/440px-Erdfunkstelle_Gran_Canaria-3.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Erdfunkstelle_Gran_Canaria-3.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Gran Canaria space tracking station</div></div></div>\n<p>In the 1960s, Gran Canaria was selected as the location for one of the 14 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ground_stations" title="Ground stations">ground stations</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Manned_Space_Flight_Network" title="Manned Space Flight Network">Manned Space Flight Network</a> (MSFN) to support the <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> space program. <a href="/wiki/Maspalomas_Station" title="Maspalomas Station">Maspalomas Station</a>, located in the south of the island, took part in a number of space missions including the <a href="/wiki/Apollo_11" title="Apollo 11">Apollo 11</a> Moon landings and <a href="/wiki/Skylab" title="Skylab">Skylab</a>. Today it continues to support satellite communications as part of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ESA" title="ESA">ESA</a> network.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-esa-page_109-0"><a href="#cite_note-esa-page-109">[109]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Because of the remote location, a number of <a href="/wiki/Observatory" title="Observatory">astronomical observatories</a> are located in the archipelago, including the <a href="/wiki/Teide_Observatory" title="Teide Observatory">Teide Observatory</a> on Tenerife, the <a href="/wiki/Roque_de_los_Muchachos_Observatory" title="Roque de los Muchachos Observatory">Roque de los Muchachos Observatory</a> on La Palma, and the <a href="/wiki/Temisas_Astronomical_Observatory" title="Temisas Astronomical Observatory">Temisas Astronomical Observatory</a> on Gran Canaria.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Canary_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RodriguezLopez2008.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" decoding="async" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/RodriguezLopez2008.jpg/200px-RodriguezLopez2008.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/RodriguezLopez2008.jpg/300px-RodriguezLopez2008.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/49/RodriguezLopez2008.jpg/400px-RodriguezLopez2008.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:RodriguezLopez2008.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Estadio_Heliodoro_Rodr%C3%ADguez_L%C3%B3pez" title="Estadio Heliodoro Rodr&#237;guez L&#243;pez">Heliodoro Rodr&#237;guez L&#243;pez Stadium</a> in Tenerife, the stadium with the largest area of field of the Canary Islands.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110"><a href="#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup></div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Estadiogc7septiembre2008.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="800" decoding="async" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Estadiogc7septiembre2008.jpg/200px-Estadiogc7septiembre2008.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Estadiogc7septiembre2008.jpg/300px-Estadiogc7septiembre2008.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Estadiogc7septiembre2008.jpg/400px-Estadiogc7septiembre2008.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Estadiogc7septiembre2008.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Estadio_Gran_Canaria" title="Estadio Gran Canaria">Gran Canaria Stadium</a>, the biggest sports venue of Canary Islands.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup></div></div></div>\n<p>A unique form of wrestling known as <a href="/wiki/Canarian_wrestling" title="Canarian wrestling">Canarian wrestling</a> (<i>lucha canaria</i>) has opponents stand in a special area called a "terrero" and try to throw each other to the ground using strength and quick movements.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ctspanish.com_113-0"><a href="#cite_note-ctspanish.com-113">[113]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Another sport is the "game of the sticks" where opponents fence with long sticks. This may have come about from the shepherds of the islands who would challenge each other using their long walking sticks.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ctspanish.com_113-1"><a href="#cite_note-ctspanish.com-113">[113]</a></sup>\n</p><p>Furthermore, there is the <a href="/wiki/Salto_del_pastor" title="Salto del pastor">shepherd\'s jump</a> (<i>salto del pastor</i>). This involves using a long stick to vault over an open area. This sport possibly evolved from the shepherd\'s need to occasionally get over an open area in the hills as they were tending their sheep.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ctspanish.com_113-2"><a href="#cite_note-ctspanish.com-113">[113]</a></sup>\n</p><p>The two main <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> teams in the archipelago are: the <a href="/wiki/CD_Tenerife" title="CD Tenerife">CD Tenerife</a> (founded in 1912) and <a href="/wiki/UD_Las_Palmas" title="UD Las Palmas">UD Las Palmas</a> (founded in 1949). As if the 2018/2019 season, both Tenerife and Las Palmas play in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Liga_Adelante" title="Liga Adelante">Liga Adelante</a>. When in the same division, the clubs contest the <a href="/wiki/Canary_Islands_derby" title="Canary Islands derby">Canary Islands derby</a>. There are smaller clubs also playing in the mainland <a href="/wiki/Spanish_football_league_system" title="Spanish football league system">Spanish football league system</a>, most notably <a href="/wiki/UD_Lanzarote" title="UD Lanzarote">UD Lanzarote</a> and <a href="/wiki/CD_Laguna_de_Tenerife" title="CD Laguna de Tenerife">CD Laguna</a>, although no other Canarian clubs have played in the top flight.\n</p><p>The mountainous terrain of the Canary Islands also caters to the growing popularity of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ultra_running" title="Ultra running">ultra running</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ultramarathons" title="Ultramarathons">ultramarathons</a> as host of annual competitive long-distance events including <a href="/wiki/Transvulcania" title="Transvulcania">Transvulcania</a> on <a href="/wiki/La_Palma" title="La Palma">La Palma</a>, Transgrancanaria<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup> on <a href="/wiki/Gran_Canaria" title="Gran Canaria">Gran Canaria</a> and the Half <a href="/wiki/Marathon_des_Sables" title="Marathon des Sables">Marathon des Sables</a> on <a href="/wiki/Fuerteventura" title="Fuerteventura">Fuerteventura</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Notable_athletes">Notable athletes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Canary_Islands&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Notable athletes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Garc%C3%ADa_(taekwondo)" title="Nicol&#225;s Garc&#237;a (taekwondo)">Nicol&#225;s Garc&#237;a</a> Hemme, born 20 June 1988 in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Las_Palmas_de_Gran_Canaria" title="Las Palmas de Gran Canaria">Las Palmas de Gran Canaria</a>, Canary Islands, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2012_London_Olympics" title="2012 London Olympics">2012 London Olympics</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taekwondo" title="Taekwondo">Taekwondo</a> Silver Medalist in Men\'s Welterweight category (&#8722;80&#160;kg).</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Cabrera" Cardinals</a> in 1913</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Sergio_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="Sergio Rodr&#237;guez">Sergio Rodr&#237;guez</a>, born in <a href="/wiki/San_Crist%C3%B3bal_de_La_Laguna" title="San Crist&#243;bal de La Laguna">San Crist&#243;bal de La Laguna</a> in 1986, played <a href="/wiki/Point_guard" title="Point guard">point guard</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Portland_Trail_Blazers" title="Portland Trail Blazers">Portland Trail Blazers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sacramento_Kings" title="Sacramento Kings">Sacramento Kings</a>, and <a href="/wiki/New_York_Knicks" title="New York Knicks">New York Knicks</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/David_Silva" title="David Silva">David Silva</a>, born in <a href="/wiki/Arguinegu%C3%ADn" title="Arguinegu&#237;n">Arguinegu&#237;n</a> in 1986, plays <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">association football</a> for <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>, member of the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> champion <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain national football team</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Carlos_Valer%C3%B3n" title="Juan Carlos Valer&#243;n">Juan Carlos Valer&#243;n</a>, born in <a href="/wiki/Arguinegu%C3%ADn" title="Deportivo de La Coru&#241;a">Deportivo la Coruna</a> and <a href="/wiki/UD_Las_Palmas" title="UD Las Palmas">Las Palmas</a></li>\n<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pedro_(footballer,_born_July_1987)" title="Pedro (footballer, born July 1987)">Pedro</a>, born in <a href="/wiki/Santa_Cruz_de_Tenerife" title="Santa Cruz de Tenerife">Santa Cruz de Tenerife</a> in 1987, plays <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">association football</a> for <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, member of the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> champion <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain national football team</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Carla_Su%C3%A1rez_Navarro" title="Carla Su&#225;rez Navarro">Carla Su&#225;rez Navarro</a>, born in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Las_Palmas_de_Gran_Canaria" title="Las Palmas de Gran Canaria">Las Palmas de Gran Canaria</a> in 1988, professional tennis player</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Paola_Tirados" title="Paola Tirados">Paola Tirados</a>, born in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Las_Palmas_de_Gran_Canaria" title="Las Palmas de Gran Canaria">Las Palmas de Gran Canaria</a> in 1980, synchronized swimmer, who participated in the Olympic Games of 2000, 2004 and 2008. She won the silver medal in Beijing in 2008 in the team competition category.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Jes%C3%A9" title="Jes&#233;">Jes&#233;</a>, born in <a class="mw-redirect" football</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stoke_City" title="Stoke City">Stoke City F.C.</a>, on loan from <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Christo_Bezuidenhout" title="Christo Bezuidenhout">Christo Bezuidenhout</a>, born in <a href="/wiki/Tenerife" title="Tenerife">Tenerife</a> in 1970, played <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">rugby union</a> for <a href="/wiki/Gloucester_Rugby" title="Gloucester Rugby">Gloucester</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Africa_national_rugby_union_team"
